[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark JSON [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector code during fuzzing tests. The vulnerability occurs in the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_string_unescape` function when processing JSON strings with Unicode surrogate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpairs, resulting in a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read operation beyond the bounds of an allocated [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m-byte heap buffer.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue represents a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread operation past the end of an allocated memory region. The overflow occurs at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress [0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[39m, which is located exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-allocated region spanning from [0m[1;36m0x50300012dcc0[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Details:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Type**: Heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mREAD operation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Severity**: SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m361:29[0m[39m` in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_string_unescape` function[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Triggering Input**: A JSON payload containing Unicode surrogate pair escape [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences: `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m\n  [0m[32m"surrogates"[0m[39m: [0m[32m"\\U0000d83d\\U0000"[0m[39m\n[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m\n\n`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Call Stack Analysis:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following execution path:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer calls `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` with the test case[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Packet dissection begins through `epan_dissect_run` and `dissect_frame`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The JSON dissector is invoked via `dissect_json`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. JSON parsing proceeds through `tvbparse_get` and callback execution[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The `after_value` callback triggers `get_json_string`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Finally, `json_string_unescape` performs the out-of-bounds read[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Memory Allocation Context:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte buffer that is overflowed was allocated through:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `wmem_strbuf_finalize` at line [0m[1;36m388[0m[39m, which calls `g_realloc`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This occurs within `get_json_string` at line [0m[1;36m564[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocation is part of string buffer finalization during JSON string [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Observations:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The input payload contains malformed Unicode escape sequences: [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\\U0000d83d\\U0000`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The second escape sequence `\\U0000` appears to be incomplete or invalid[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The overflow occurs when processing these Unicode surrogate pairs[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m19[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m suggests it contains the partially processed string [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The read operation occurs at the exact boundary of the allocated region, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating the code attempts to read one character beyond the finalized string[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Areas Requiring Investigation:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo understand this vulnerability comprehensively, the following code sections [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m` - specifically the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_string_unescape` function around line [0m[1;36m361[0m                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unicode escape sequence handling, particularly for surrogate pairs[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **String Buffer Management:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/wsutil/wmem/[0m[95mwmem_strbuf.c[0m[39m` - the `wmem_strbuf_finalize` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m of `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m`. The root cause is [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-standard `\U` + `\U` escape sequence pattern.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Details[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **The Vulnerable Code Path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m353[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m378[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When a lead surrogate is detected from a `\U` escape sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\U0000d83d` → [0m[1;36m0xd83d[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - And followed by another `\U` escape for the trail surrogate[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The loop at lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m attempts to read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits **without bounds [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m: `current_character = string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mread_index[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` reads beyond the buffer[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Grammar vs Implementation Mismatch:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Grammar [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1312[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m accepts only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits for both `\u` and `\U`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Code expects [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits for `\U` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m359[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input `\U0000d83d\U0000` has incomplete second escape [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m digits provided[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parser accepts it as valid, but unescape tries to read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m digits[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Code Inconsistency:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `\U` + `\u` case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m313[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m352[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **has proper bounds checking** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m322[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m326[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `\u` + `\u` case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m466[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m504[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **has proper bounds checking** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m475[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `\U` + `\U` case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m353[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m378[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **lacks bounds checking** - this is the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbug[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m multi-byte character handling** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m197[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m217[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Standard escape sequences** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m231[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m388[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m414[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Initial `\U` parsing** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m262[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m291[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - has correct bounds checking[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Surrogate pair validation and combination** using `IS_LEAD_SURROGATE`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IS_TRAIL_SURROGATE`, `SURROGATE_VALUE` macros[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **String buffer management** - must not break memory allocation/deallocation[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Bounds Checking to `\U` + `\U` Surrogate Pair Handling[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m` lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Add bounds checking inside the loop** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore line [0m[1;36m361[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnibble < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           break;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       trail_surrogate <<= [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       trail_surrogate |= nibble;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m341[0m[39m: `\U` + `\u` surrogate pair parsing  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m422[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m444[0m[39m: Initial `\u` parsing[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m472[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[39m: `\u` + `\u` surrogate pair parsing[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Locate the buggy loop**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Context: Inside `else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent_character == [0m[32m'U'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m353[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Set `is_valid_unicode_character = false` when bounds exceeded[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `break` out of the loop to prevent further reads[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add hex digit validation**[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Set `is_valid_unicode_character = false` for invalid hex digits[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `break` out of the loop to prevent corrupted data[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Verify error handling**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing code at lines [0m[1;36m375[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m already handles `is_valid_unicode_character = [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse`[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing code at lines [0m[1;36m410[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m413[0m[39m already appends replacement character for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid sequences[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes needed to error handling logic[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change:** Only adds bounds checking to the one location that's missing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistency:** Makes the code consistent with all other similar loops in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame function[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Logic:** Doesn't change the surrogate pair handling algorithm[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fail-Safe:** Gracefully handles malformed input by setting error flag and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbreaking[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes:** Maintains compatibility with existing valid inputs[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Standard Pattern:** Uses the same bounds checking pattern already established [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the codebase[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Surrogate Pair Handling:** The `SURROGATE_VALUE` macro combination still works[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor valid inputs[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error Recovery:** Invalid sequences already trigger replacement character [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsertion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m412[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m539[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Buffer Management:** No changes to `wmem_strbuf` operations[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Grammar Compatibility:** Still accepts the same grammar tokens, just validates[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem better[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Other Escape Sequences:** No impact on `\u`, `\n`, `\t`, etc.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Vulnerability[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents Buffer Overflow:** Bounds check stops reading past buffer end[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Handles Incomplete Sequences:** Gracefully fails when fewer than [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Validates Input:** Hex digit check catches non-hex characters[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Safe Failure Mode:** Sets error flag instead of crashing[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Replacement Character:** Invalid sequences result in � [0m[1;39m([0m[39mU+FFFD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in output[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m:** Incomplete `\U` sequences now result in replacement character [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of crash[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** This is correct behavior - invalid input should not crash the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact:** Improves robustness for malformed JSON[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m:** Grammar still accepts `\U` with [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m digits, but unescape expects [0m[1;36m8[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** Bounds check catches this mismatch and handles it safely[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact:** No crash, replacement character inserted [0m[1;39m([0m[39macceptable behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Future Enhancement:** Could update grammar to require [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m digits for `\U`, but [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot necessary for security fix[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m:** Non-standard `\U` support is retained[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** This appears intentional [0m[1;39m([0m[39msupports direct Unicode code points vs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate pairs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact:** No change to existing functionality for valid `\U` sequences[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Note:** Standard JSON only supports `\uXXXX`, but Wireshark extends this[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m291[0m[39m:** Initial `\U` parsing - has identical bounds checking pattern[0m  [2m                [0m
